<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">kanał</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">canale</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">canalis</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">canna</i>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κάννα</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kánna</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:канава.html>кана́ва</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kanáva</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:канава.html>кана́вы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:канава.html>кана́вы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:канава.html>кана́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>ditch, gutter, drain, trench</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:канализация.html>канализа́ция</a> (13023)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:канализация.html>канализа́ция</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kanalizácija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:канализация.html>канализа́ции</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:канализация.html>канализа́ции</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:канализация.html>канализа́ций</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:канализационный.html>канализацио́нный</a></b>)

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кандидат.html>кандида́т</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kandidát</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кандидат.html>кандида́та</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кандидат.html>кандида́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кандидат.html>кандида́тов</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кандидатка.html>кандида́тка</a></b>)

***каникулы.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:каникулы.html>кани́кулы</a> (6669)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From the Latin <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">Canicula</i>, meaning "small dog", an alternative name of the star Sirius, which from the 24th of July to the 24th of August rises and sets at the same time as the sun, thus concerning this summer period. See <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">dog days</i> for more information.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:каникулы.html>кани́кулы</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kaníkuly</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> <abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:каникулы.html>кани́кул</a></b>, <i>plural only</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>(school, university, parliament) vacation <i>(U.S.)</i>, holiday <i>(UK)</i></li></ol>

***канитель.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:канитель.html>каните́ль</a> (26335)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">cannetille</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es">cañutillo</i>, diminutive of <i class="Latn mention" lang="es">cañuto</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mozarabic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Mozarabic language">Mozarabic</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">canna</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κάννα</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kánna</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Akkadian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Akkadian language">Akkadian</a></span> <i class="Xsux mention" lang="akk">𒄀</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="akk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">qanû</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sumerian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Sumerian language">Sumerian</a></span> <i class="Xsux mention" lang="sux">𒄀𒈾</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sux-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gi.na</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:канитель.html>каните́ль</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kanitélʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:канитель.html>каните́ли</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:канитель.html>каните́ли</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:канитель.html>каните́лей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">jewelry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> thin metallic gold or silver thread, used for embroidery or decoration</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> protracted, tedious affair, waste of time</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:канон.html>кано́н</a></span> «<a href = vnd.unilang:звездный.html>Звёздного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:путь.html>пути́</a>» <a href = vnd.unilang:входить.html>вхо́дят</a> «<a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>все</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:событие.html>собы́тия</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сериал.html>сериа́лов</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:фильм.html>фи́льмов</a>». <a href = vnd.unilang:соответственно.html>Соотве́тственно</a>, неканонично <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:остальной.html>остально́е</a>: <a href = vnd.unilang:сопутствующий.html>сопу́тствующие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:роман.html>рома́ны</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:комикс.html>ко́миксы</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:игра.html>игры</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мультфильм.html>мультфи́льмы</a>. </span></li>

***кануть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кануть.html>ка́нуть</a> (13412)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kapnǫti</i>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:капнуть.html>ка́пнуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kápnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кануть.html>ка́нуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kánutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to fall, to sink</li>
<li>to disappear, to vanish
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кануть.html>ка́нуть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вечность.html>ве́чность</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kánutʹ</b> v véčnostʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">fall/sink into oblivion</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вода.html>во́ду</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:кануть.html>ка́нуть</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kak v vódu <b>kánutʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to disappear/vanish without a trace; vanish into thin air</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:канцлер.html>ка́нцлер</a> (15074)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Kanzler</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:канцлер.html>ка́нцлер</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">káncler</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:канцлер.html>ка́нцлера</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:канцлер.html>ка́нцлеры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:канцлер.html>ка́нцлеров</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ка́нцлерша</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>chancellor <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">head of parliamentary government in some German speaking countries</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The feminine form "канцлерша" is considered too colloquial and the masculine form "<a href = vnd.unilang:канцлер.html>ка́нцлер</a>" is used for both male and female chancellors.</li></ul>

vnd.unilang:смотреть.html>смотре́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:новинка.html>нови́нки</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мода.html>мо́ды</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:духота.html>духоты́</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:кондиционер.html>кондиционе́ры</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Xočú ostanovítʹsja na krúpnyx torgóvyx kómpleksax, <b>kanʹónax</b>, kak ix zdesʹ nazyvájut. <b>Kanʹón</b> — ogrómnyj magazín pod krýšej — ljubímoje mésto progúlok i razvlečénij. Po provedennomu análizu 28 procéntov xódjat v <b>kanʹón</b> ne dlja pokúpki, a tak — sebjá pokazátʹ, drugíx posmotrétʹ. Vpervýje <b>kanʹóny</b> stáli stroitʹ v Amerike. V Izraile oní privilisʹ ješčó po odnój pričíne: prijátno guljátʹ, smotrétʹ novínki módy i vse éto bez žarý i duxotý — kondicionéry.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I want to stop at the large shopping complexes—<b>malls, or kanyons</b>, as they are called here. A <b>mall</b> is a large store under a roof, a favorite place for walking and entertainment. According to a study that was done, 28 percent go to the <b>mall</b> not for shopping, but just for fun—to show off, to look at others. <b>Malls</b> were first built in America. In Israel, they appeared for another reason: It feels nice to walk around, look at the new fads—and all this without the heat and humidity: air conditioners.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li>

***канючивший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:канючить.html>каню́чивший</a> (22522)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:канючить.html>каню́чить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kanjúčitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>

<ol><li>to pester with requests, to moan, to grumble</li></ol>

***капать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:капать.html>ка́пать</a> (7381)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:капать.html>ка́пать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kápatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:капнуть.html>ка́пнуть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:накапать.html>нака́пать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to drip, to drop, to spill</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to squeal, to inform, to dob</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:капелла.html>капе́лла</a> (15753)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">cappella</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:капелла.html>капе́лла</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kapɛ́lla</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:капелла.html>капе́ллы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:капелла.html>капе́ллы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:капелла.html>капе́лл</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>choir of singers <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">from the 18th century,  mixed ensemble of singers and musicians</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>

<li>chapel</li>
